msg:This is the first time in so many years that I have encountered so many problems when staying in a hotel. The hotel was randomly selected. After dinner, it looked close. When parking, there were two parking spaces with normal lines, but the length was actually far from enough. Fortunately, my car had a collision warning, otherwise the rear bumper would have been against the wall. I suggest that the hotel make a reminder for this parking space. The takeaway I ordered after checking in arrived at the hotel around 10 o'clock. The takeaway guy couldn't get into the passenger elevator. I understood that at that time, I had taken a shower and changed into pajamas. I wanted to contact the front desk to see if the robot or manual delivery was sent up, and told me to come down to pick it up myself. After many negotiations, it was not possible. Then I could only change clothes and go down to pick it up. This experience was also quite speechless. I slept until almost three o'clock at night, and woke up. I was awakened by the sound of water on the top of the bathroom. I think my sleep is not that shallow. The sound continued until about five o'clock. There may be more later, but I was too sleepy to fall asleep at that time. I got up at eight o'clock in the morning to pack my things, and accidentally found that there were things behind the bedside table that were not mine. It felt like underwear. With this hygiene situation, I think I have to question whether towels and cups can be replaced and disinfected for each guest! The last breakfast was not as good as the breakfast I had at Hanting ten years ago. There was basically no hot food before 8:30. The dining area was large but there was not much food on offer. I had no appetite at all. In the end, I had some fried rice, two small pieces of crispy meat, and a cup of yogurt. Not to mention how high the starch content of the crispy meat was, I couldn't accept it when I put it in my mouth and found that it was cold! ! When I left the restaurant, I reminded the handsome guy who collected the meal coupons that the dish was cold, but he didn't seem to react. There were also front desk staff who took the food like the guests, sat in the restaurant to eat, and then went to work at the front desk (when I went to the front desk to ask about the parking coupons, I found that I met them in the restaurant).
How to say it? It's outrageous, quite outrageous, outrageous to the point of outrageous! The management team of this hotel has a long way to go, so take care of yourself.
